< review>
I will NEVER go to this place again. I got my front brakes done in October 2013, when I reviewed the work with the manager, I asked him about the back brakes just to be told that the back brakes were at 80% and did NOT need to be changed and that I had at least 6 months to a year to go until they needed to be replaced. Not more than a week later, my back brakes go out, I return my car to them and they tell me that my back brakes went out because I had "driven with my emergency brake on." You can't move this car with the brake down. He said that my calipers had been stuck in the down position and that I had to replace the roters (because they don't have the tools to resurface roters) and replace the brake pads and the calipers. Total cost at that point was over $500.00 (this is in addition to what I had already paid for the front brakes of over $300.00). I had no choice but to let them do the work. When I returned to pick up my car, all of a sudden, there was another "issue" with the car. They had stated that there was an oil leak from an oil line that had to be replaced which ran me $135.00. I had not been previously called to be informed of this being needed, I had a working phone so there was no excuse to why I was not previously informed instead I get told when I arrive and then had to wait over an hour while that work was done.
Less than 6 months later, I yet again have issues with my brakes. My friend takes the car to another place and they tell him that all 4 brakes are shot, the brake pads are worn down to the CORE, everything has to be replaced AGAIN!!! Then I am informed that this place uses "Organic Brake Pads" which don't have the same metal as traditional brake pads which cause them to wear down a lot faster, this is information NEVER relayed to me verbally or in writing.
I don't drive long distances and I don't ride my brakes and I don't have a need to slam on my brakes so there is no reason that these brakes and brake pads should be worn down to metal after LESS than 6 months of being newly installed.

Don't go to this place, you'll only be wasting your money and time.<//review>

Not more than a week later, my back brakes go out, I return my car to them and they tell me that my back brakes went out because I had "driven with my emergency brake on." You can't move this car with the brake down. He said that my calipers had been stuck in the down position and that I had to replace the roters (because they don't have the tools to resurface roters) and replace the brake pads and the calipers. Total cost at that point was over $500.00 (this is in addition to what I had already paid for the front brakes of over $300.00). I had no choice but to let them do the work. When I returned to pick up my car, all of a sudden, there was another "issue" with the car. They had stated that there was an oil leak from an oil line that had to be replaced which ran me $135.00. I had not been previously called to be informed of this being needed, I had a working phone so there was no excuse to why I was not previously informed instead I get told when I arrive and then had to wait over an hour while that work was done.
Less than 6 months later, I yet again have issues with my brakes. My friend takes the car to another place and they tell him that all 4 brakes are shot, the brake pads are worn down to the CORE, everything has to be replaced AGAIN!!! Then I am informed that this place uses "Organic Brake Pads" which don't have the same metal as traditional brake pads which cause them to wear down a lot faster, this is information NEVER relayed to me verbally or in writing.
I don't drive long distances and I don't ride my brakes and I don't have a need to slam on my brakes so there is no reason that these brakes and brake pads should be worn down to metal after LESS than 6 months of being newly installed.

Don't go to this place, you'll only be wasting your money and time.</Text>

<user>106484591046630285343< /user><Name>Rene Cortez<//Name><date>1509379980748< /date>< rating>

< Review>
We were in an epic battle against a never-ending army of ants that had raged for several days. At first it was a few ants and we easily got rid of them. Then more would show up but we did the same thing. There were times we thought we won only to soon realize that we in over our heads as more and more ants kept showing up.

So I Yelped an extermination company and several dozen popped up. I read tons of reviews and requested quotes using Yelp's feature. All of them responded but their approach varied and didn't come off friendly, professional,  or knowledgeable. As a matter of fact, some people were pretty vague. They would say things like, "it depends" or "we need to have someone come out to inspect" or "we don't service that area" even though their office was less than 5 miles from our home.

Pro Pacific Pest Control was the outlier. I called after 6 p.m. knowing that they were closed according to Yelp hoping that someone would answer. And Mike did! He was friendly, professional, and knowledgeable. He was not vague in the least. On the contrary, he explained their services and pricing and even recommended one based on what I told him.

He said he would have someone come out the next morning between 10 a.m. and 1 p.m. and James showed up at 10:15 a.m. He even called to let me know when he was on his way. James was very cool and friendly. He did a great job explaining how and why he was treating certain areas for the ants and other pests like silverfish and wasps. Sadly he works in the Inland Empire so we won't see him again. I hope that the next technician is just as great. I'm fairly certain based on the service from Mike and James that I will be satisfied.

As far as the ants are concerned, they became like Houdini. Poof! All gone. The next day I saw dead crickets around the house and a few spiders, too. I am extremely satisfied with the experience so far and as long as the service continues, it should remain this way.</Review>

<Time>1516485907287< /Time><Rate>4</Rate>< Review>
Clean and organized thrift shop. The prices here are higher than other stores like Goodwill but the quality also tends to be higher. Expect to find some designer brands mixed in, and lots of interesting pieces. They offer returns on clothing only, for a few days after purchase if you keep your receipt. Note that you will receive store credit, not cash or refund.

The biggest downside is that there are no fitting rooms. If they changed that I would give them 5 stars.< /Review>

<Name>Larkin Cypher</Name>< text>
Some of the best deals in town on produce, frozen, and snack food. They usually have enough help on the registers to move you through quickly. the staff is friendly, helpful, and cool. <userid>111039560162694224214</userid>< Text>
I have heard good things about these places, so since we were fairly nearby my wife and I decided to check it out.  They do have decent prices, but of course you need to know what the items would cost regularly to be able to tell exactly how good a deal you are getting. We have a nearby Frazier Market that always has great prices on produce, and my wife said their prices are about the same for fruits and veggies. They also get a few interesting vegan items, but from what I understand it is kind of hit-or-miss. If you have one of these Grocery Outlets near you it is probably great, but I don't think I would want to do a long drive just to find out they don't have much that I am interested in. Today they had a few vegan ice creams at great prices, so I was a happy camper.  As others have said, they do have a decent selection of wines. There is also plenty of parking, and the store personnel seemed friendly enough.</Text>
